// ── NAV
function nav(btn,id){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('on'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.pg').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('on'));
  btn.classList.add('on');document.getElementById(id).classList.add('on');
}
function navTo(pgId){
  const map={'visao':'pg-visao','churn':'pg-churn','imobs':'pg-imobs','usuarios':'pg-usuarios','cob':'pg-cob'};
  const tabs=document.querySelectorAll('.tab');
  const ids=['visao','churn','imobs','usuarios','cob'];
  const idx=ids.indexOf(pgId); if(idx<0)return;
  tabs.forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('on'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.pg').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('on'));
  tabs[idx].classList.add('on');
  document.getElementById(map[pgId]).classList.add('on');
}
document.getElementById('nav-date').textContent='maio/2026 · atualizado '+D.gerado;

// Pills drill-down
let chFilters={motivo:null, forma:null, faixa:null};
let chP=1; const CH_PG=40;

function makePills(containerId, data, filterKey, colors){
  const total=Object.values(data).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
  document.getElementById(containerId).innerHTML=Object.entries(data).map(([k,v])=>`
    <div class="pill${chFilters[filterKey]===k?' active':''}" onclick="toggleFilter('${filterKey}','${k.replace(/'/g,"\'")}')">
      <span class="pill-n">${v}</span>
      <span class="pill-l">${k}</span>
    </div>`).join('');
}

function buildPills(){
  makePills('pills-motivo', CH.por_motivo, 'motivo');
  makePills('pills-forma',  CH.por_forma,  'forma');
  makePills('pills-faixa',  CH.por_faixa,  'faixa');
}
buildPills();

function toggleFilter(key, val){
  chFilters[key] = chFilters[key]===val ? null : val;
  buildPills(); renderChurnList();
}
function clearFilters(){
  chFilters={motivo:null,forma:null,faixa:null};
  buildPills(); renderChurnList();
  document.getElementById('ch-q').value='';
}

function getChurnFiltered(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('ch-q').value||'').toLowerCase();
  return CH.lista.filter(c=>{
    if(chFilters.motivo && c.motivo!==chFilters.motivo) return false;
    if(chFilters.forma  && c.forma!==chFilters.forma)   return false;
    if(chFilters.faixa  && c.faixa!==chFilters.faixa)   return false;
    if(q && !c.nome.toLowerCase().includes(q) && !c.email.toLowerCase().includes(q) && !c.imob.toLowerCase().includes(q)) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

function renderChurnList(){
  const list=getChurnFiltered(), pages=Math.ceil(list.length/CH_PG)||1;
  const slice=list.slice((chP-1)*CH_PG, chP*CH_PG);
  const ativos=[chFilters.motivo,chFilters.forma,chFilters.faixa].filter(Boolean);
  document.getElementById('drill-info').textContent=
    ativos.length ? `${list.length} resultados · filtros: ${ativos.join(' + ')}` : `${list.length} churns total`;
  document.getElementById('ch-info').textContent=`${chP}/${pages}`;
  document.getElementById('ch-prev').disabled=chP<=1;
  document.getElementById('ch-next').disabled=chP>=pages;
  document.getElementById('churn-body').innerHTML=slice.map(c=>`
    <tr onclick='openUser(${JSON.stringify({...c,status:"Churn"})})' style="cursor:pointer">
      <td class="w" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${c.nome||'—'}</td>
      <td class="w" style="font-size:11px">${c.imob||'—'}</td>
      <td class="m">${c.plano||'—'}</td>
      <td class="m">${c.valor?'R$ '+c.valor.toFixed(0):'—'}</td>
      <td><span class="badge churn" style="white-space:normal">${c.motivo||'—'}</span></td>
      <td>${forma_b(c.forma)}</td>
      <td class="m">${c.periodo?c.periodo+'m':'—'}</td>
      <td class="m">${c.mes_ch||'—'}</td>
    </tr>`).join('');
}
renderChurnList();

// ── IMOBILIÁRIAS
function renderImobs(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('iq').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const s=document.getElementById('isort').value;
  const f=document.getElementById('ifilt').value;
  let list=D.imob_list.filter(i=>{
    if(!i.nome.toLowerCase().includes(q)) return false;
    if(f==='remax'&&!i.nome.toLowerCase().includes('remax')) return false;
    if(f==='alta'&&i.conv<50) return false;
    if(f==='risco'&&i.churn<=i.assin) return false;
    return true;
  });
  list.sort((a,b)=>s==='nome'?a.nome.localeCompare(b.nome):(b[s]||0)-(a[s]||0));
  document.getElementById('i-count').textContent=list.length;
  const maxT=Math.max(...list.map(i=>i.total));
  document.getElementById('i-body').innerHTML=list.map(i=>{
    const cor=i.conv>=60?'var(--green)':i.conv>=30?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)';
    return `<tr onclick='openImob(${JSON.stringify(i)})' style="cursor:pointer">
      <td class="w" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${i.nome}</td>
      <td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px">
        <div style="width:${Math.round(i.total/maxT*40)}px;height:3px;background:var(--blue-l);border-radius:2px"></div>
        <span class="m">${i.total}</span></div></td>
      <td class="m" style="color:var(--green);font-weight:600">${i.assin}</td>
      <td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px">
        <div style="width:40px;height:5px;background:var(--paper3);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden">
          <div style="width:${Math.min(i.conv,100)}%;height:100%;background:${cor};border-radius:3px"></div></div>
        <span class="m" style="color:${cor};font-weight:600">${i.conv}%</span></div></td>
      <td class="m" style="color:var(--blue)">${i.pot}</td>
      <td class="m" style="color:var(--red)">${i.churn}</td>
      <td class="m" style="color:var(--amber)">${i.trial}</td>
      <td class="m" style="color:${i.atraso>0?'var(--amber)':'var(--ink4)'}">${i.atraso}</td>
    </tr>`;}).join('');
}
renderImobs();

// ── USUÁRIOS
let uP=1; const U_PG=50;
function getUsrs(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('uq').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const st=document.getElementById('ust').value;
  const im=document.getElementById('uimob').value;
  const fo=document.getElementById('uforma').value;
  return D.usuarios.filter(u=>
    (!q||u.nome.toLowerCase().includes(q)||u.email.toLowerCase().includes(q)||u.imob.toLowerCase().includes(q))&&
    (!st||u.status===st)&&(!im||u.imob===im)&&(!fo||u.forma===fo));
}
function renderUsr(reset){
  if(reset) uP=1;
  const list=getUsrs(), pages=Math.ceil(list.length/U_PG)||1;
  const slice=list.slice((uP-1)*U_PG, uP*U_PG);
  document.getElementById('u-count').textContent=list.length.toLocaleString('pt-BR');
  document.getElementById('u-info').textContent=`${uP}/${pages}`;
  document.getElementById('u-prev').disabled=uP<=1;
  document.getElementById('u-next').disabled=uP>=pages;
  document.getElementById('u-body').innerHTML=slice.map(u=>{
    const dc=u.dias!==null&&u.dias<0?'var(--red)':u.dias!==null&&u.dias<=7?'var(--amber)':'var(--ink3)';
    const dt=u.dias===null?'—':u.dias<0?Math.abs(u.dias)+'d atrs':u.dias+'d';
    return `<tr onclick='openUser(${JSON.stringify(u)})' style="cursor:pointer">
      <td class="w" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${u.nome||'—'}</td>
      <td class="m" style="color:var(--ink3);max-width:170px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${u.email}</td>
      <td class="w" style="font-size:11px">${u.imob||'—'}</td>
      <td class="m">${u.plano||'—'}</td>
      <td>${forma_b(u.forma)}</td>
      <td class="m">${u.valor?'R$ '+u.valor.toFixed(0):'—'}</td>
      <td class="m">${u.vence||'—'}</td>
      <td class="m" style="color:${dc};font-weight:600">${dt}</td>
    </tr>`;}).join('');
}
const imobsSet=[...new Set(D.usuarios.map(u=>u.imob).filter(Boolean))].sort();
const usel=document.getElementById('uimob');
imobsSet.forEach(i=>{const o=document.createElement('option');o.value=i;o.textContent=i;usel.appendChild(o);});
renderUsr(1);

    <td class="w" style="font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${u.nome||'—'}</td>
    <td class="w" style="font-size:11px">${u.imob||'—'}</td>
    <td class="m" style="color:${cor};font-weight:700">${u.dias}d</td>
    <td class="m">${u.vence}</td>
    <td>${wpp(u.wpp)}</td>
  </tr>`;}).join('');

// ── MODAL
function openUser(u){
  const dc=u.dias!==null&&u.dias<=0?'var(--red)':u.dias!==null&&u.dias<=7?'var(--amber)':'var(--ink)';
  const dt=u.dias===null?'—':u.dias<0?`Vencido há ${Math.abs(u.dias)}d ⚠️`:u.dias===0?'Vence hoje ⚠️':`Vence em ${u.dias}d`;
  const rows=[
    ['Status',`<span class="badge ${bc(u.status||'Churn')}">${u.status||'Churn'}</span>`],
    ['Imobiliária',u.imob||'—'],
    ['WhatsApp',u.wpp?`<a href="https://wa.me/55${u.wpp.replace(/\D/g,'')}" target="_blank" style="color:var(--green)">${u.wpp}</a>`:'—'],
    ['Plano',u.plano||'—'],
    ['Forma pgto',u.forma||'—'],
    ['Valor',u.valor?'R$ '+u.valor.toFixed(2):'—'],
  ];
  if(u.status==='Churn'||u.motivo){
    rows.push(['Motivo churn',u.motivo||'—'],['Permanência',u.periodo?u.periodo+'m':'—'],['Mês churn',u.mes_ch||'—']);
  } else {
    rows.push(['Plano válido até',u.vence||'—'],['Situação',`<span style="color:${dc}">${dt}</span>`]);
    if(u.meses!==undefined&&u.meses!==null) rows.push(['Meses como assinante',u.meses+'m']);
  }
  openModal(`<h2>${u.nome||'Sem nome'}</h2>
    <div style="color:var(--ink3);font-size:12px;font-family:var(--mono);margin-top:2px">${u.email}</div>
    <div style="margin-top:14px">${rows.map(([k,v])=>`
      <div class="mrow"><span class="mkey">${k}</span><span class="mval">${v}</span></div>`).join('')}
    </div>`);
}

function openImob(i){
  const cor=i.conv>=60?'var(--green)':i.conv>=30?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)';
  const usrs=D.usuarios.filter(u=>u.imob===i.nome).slice(0,10);
  const churnsImob=CH.lista.filter(c=>c.imob===i.nome).slice(0,5);
  openModal(`<h2>${i.nome}</h2>
    <div style="margin-top:12px">
      ${[['Total usuários',i.total],['Assinantes ativos',`<span style="color:var(--green);font-weight:600">${i.assin}</span>`],
         ['Conversão',`<span style="color:${cor};font-weight:600">${i.conv}%</span>`],
         ['Potencial',`<span style="color:var(--blue)">${i.pot}</span>`],
         ['Churn histórico',`<span style="color:var(--red)">${i.churn}</span>`],
         ['Atraso/Falha',`<span style="color:${i.atraso>0?'var(--amber)':'var(--ink)'}">${i.atraso}</span>`],
        ].map(([k,v])=>`<div class="mrow"><span class="mkey">${k}</span><span class="mval">${v}</span></div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    ${usrs.length?`<div class="msec">Assinantes (${usrs.length})</div>
      <div class="musers">${usrs.map(u=>`
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--line);cursor:pointer" onclick="openUser(${JSON.stringify(u)})">
          <span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600">${u.nome||'—'}</span>
          <span>${forma_b(u.forma)}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}</div>`:''}
    ${churnsImob.length?`<div class="msec">Churns recentes</div>
      <div class="musers">${churnsImob.map(c=>`
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--line);cursor:pointer" onclick="openUser(${JSON.stringify(c)})">
          <span style="font-size:12px">${c.nome||'—'}</span>
          <span class="badge churn">${c.motivo||'—'}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}</div>`:''}
    `);
}

function openModal(html){
  document.getElementById('mbody').innerHTML=html;
  document.getElementById('ov').classList.add('open');
}
function closeModal(){document.getElementById('ov').classList.remove('open');}
document.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Escape')closeModal();});
</script>

<div id="loading" style="display:none;position:fixed;bottom:20px;right:20px;background:#0f0f0f;color:#fff;padding:10px 16px;border-radius:8px;font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;font-size:12px;z-index:300">
  ↻ Atualizando...
</div>
<div id="toast" style="position:fixed;bottom:20px;left:20px;background:#1a7a4a;color:#fff;padding:10px 16px;border-radius:8px;font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;font-size:12px;z-index:300;display:none">
</div>
<script>
const DATA_URL = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/treinamentononstop/nonstop-dashboard/main/data.json';
// Tentar buscar dados atualizados do GitHub no carregamento
(async function() {
  try {
    const r = await fetch(DATA_URL + '?v=' + Date.now());
    if (!r.ok) return;
    const newD = await r.json();
    // Mostrar toast com data de atualização
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
    toast.textContent = '✅ Dados de ' + (newD.gerado || '');
    toast.style.display = 'block';
    setTimeout(() => toast.style.display = 'none', 4000);
    console.log('Dados atualizados do GitHub:', newD.gerado);
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('Usando dados locais (offline ou primeiro acesso)');
  }
})();

// Botão de atualização manual
function recarregarDados() {
  location.reload();
}
</script>
</body>
</html>
